#--------------------------------------------------
echo "CPM Filter Router and Svc-id Match Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    system
        security
            cpm-filter
                ip-filter
                    no shutdown
                    entry 320
                        match protocol icmp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 600
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 601
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 608
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 609
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
